## <a name="windows-server-2008"></a><span data-ttu-id="cffa9-446">Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cffa9-446">Windows Server 2008</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="cffa9-447">Attributs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cffa9-447">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2008-attributes)

## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="cffa9-1230">Attributs Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cffa9-1230">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cffa9-1231">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2012 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cffa9-1231">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
